),
metadata={"selfplay": False},
)
def main(config_path: str | Path = "athenachka2.train.yaml") -> None:
cfg = load_train_config(config_path)
backend = NoOpBackend()
orch = TrainerOrchestrator(cfg, backend=backend)
# Continuous ingest
for i in range(3):
report = orch.continuous_ingest(demo_sample(f"packet.demo.{i}"), epoch=i)
print("INGEST", i, report)
# Episode-end scheduler hook
obs = SchedulerObservation(
episodes_seen=500,
proofs_completed=1000,
wall_time_seconds=3600.0,
gpu_dollars=1.0,
watt_hours=500.0,
ram_gib_hours=12.0,
vram_util=0.55,
divergent_kernel_fraction=0.01,
idle_kernel_fraction=0.02,
hot_shelf_ids=["root.route"],
)
hook = orch.on_episode_end(obs)
print("SCHEDULER_HOOK", hook)
# Hourly / nightly / weekly
print("HOURLY", orch.hourly_maintenance(nvme_free_gb=8.0))
print("NIGHTLY", orch.nightly_cycle())
print("WEEKLY", orch.weekly_cycle())
if __name__ == "__main__":
main()
This is the first place where the whole system actually behaves like one organism instead of separate sketches: ingest verifies and appends exceptions, the scheduler can change compute topology without owning truth, the distiller can promote stable shelves without bypassing witness/replay law, and the nightly / weekly loops consume the exact route-packet buffers you defined earlier. That preserves the main invariant in your docs: compute/storage adaptation is allowed, but truth, promotion, and learning remain subordinate to witness, replay, and corridor closure.
The next strongest layer is the actual models.py / backend_hf.py bridge: PEFT-wrapped Phi limbs, freeze masks applied from optimizer_groups.py, and phase-specific run_phase() implementations for SFT, SPIN, GRPO, and tool-negative replay.
This is the concrete Hugging Face bridge.
The key implementation choices are grounded in two things. First, your corpus insists on an immutable/frozen invariant substrate with plastic adapters, observer heads, planner/verifier/mode/scheduler organs, and route-packets as the atomic training object. Second, the current Hugging Face stack supports exactly the right outer shape: PEFT/QLoRA uses BitsAndBytesConfig + prepare_model_for_kbit_training() + LoraConfig; TRL exposes SFTTrainer and GRPOTrainer; Transformers Trainer is explicitly meant to be subclassed when you need a custom compute_loss(); and Phi-4-multimodal can be loaded with AutoProcessor + AutoModelForCausalLM, with its vision/speech adapters loaded separately. (Hugging Face)
Because TRL currently gives you SFT and GRPO as first-class trainers but not a dedicated “SPIN trainer,” the SPIN phase below is implemented as a custom pairwise trainer on top of transformers.Trainer, using the documented custom compute_loss() extension point. (Hugging Face)
models.py
from __future__ import annotations
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict, Iterable, List, Literal, Optional, Sequence
import warnings
import torch
from transformers import (
AutoModelForCausalLM,
AutoProcessor,
AutoTokenizer,
BitsAndBytesConfig,
)
from peft import (
LoraConfig,
TaskType,
get_peft_model,
prepare_model_for_kbit_training,
)
from config_schema import TrainConfig
from optimizer_groups import apply_freeze_masks, report_parameter_groups
Role = Literal["planner", "perception", "verifier", "scheduler"]
@dataclass
class LimbBundle:
role: Role
model_name: str
model: torch.nn.Module
tokenizer: Optional[object] = None
processor: Optional[object] = None
modality: Literal["text", "multimodal"] = "text"
adapter_name: str = "default"
parameter_report: Optional[dict] = None
def _torch_dtype(dtype_name: str) -> torch.dtype:
if dtype_name == "bf16":
return torch.bfloat16
if dtype_name == "fp16":
return torch.float16
return torch.float32
def build_quantization_config(cfg: TrainConfig) -> Optional[BitsAndBytesConfig]:
if not cfg.precision.qlora_4bit:
return None
return BitsAndBytesConfig(
load_in_4bit=True,
bnb_4bit_quant_type=cfg.precision.qlora_quant_type,
bnb_4bit_use_double_quant=cfg.precision.qlora_double_quant,
bnb_4bit_compute_dtype=_torch_dtype(cfg.precision.train_dtype),
)
def choose_lora_rank_alpha(
cfg: TrainConfig,
heavy: bool = False,
) -> tuple[int, int]:
if heavy:
return cfg.peft.rank_heavy, cfg.peft.alpha_heavy
return cfg.peft.rank_small, cfg.peft.alpha_small
def make_lora_config(
cfg: TrainConfig,
*,
heavy: bool = False,
target_modules: Optional[Sequence[str]] = None,
modules_to_save: Optional[Sequence[str]] = None,
) -> LoraConfig:
rank, alpha = choose_lora_rank_alpha(cfg, heavy=heavy)
return LoraConfig(
task_type=TaskType.CAUSAL_LM,
inference_mode=False,
r=rank,
lora_alpha=alpha,
lora_dropout=cfg.peft.lora_dropout,
bias=cfg.peft.bias,
target_modules=list(target_modules) if target_modules is not None else list(cfg.peft.target_modules_small),
modules_to_save=list(modules_to_save) if modules_to_save is not None else None,
)
def _maybe_set_pad_token(tokenizer) -> None:
if getattr(tokenizer, "pad_token", None) is None and getattr(tokenizer, "eos_token", None) is not None:
tokenizer.pad_token = tokenizer.eos_token
def _attach_adapter(
model: torch.nn.Module,
adapter_name: str,
lora_config: LoraConfig,
) -> torch.nn.Module:
"""
Prefer Transformers/PEFT adapter integration if available.
Fallback to get_peft_model if add_adapter is unavailable.
"""
try:
if hasattr(model, "add_adapter"):
model.add_adapter(lora_config, adapter_name=adapter_name)
if hasattr(model, "set_adapter"):
model.set_adapter(adapter_name)
return model
except Exception as exc:  # pragma: no cover
warnings.warn(f"add_adapter() failed for adapter={adapter_name}: {exc}; falling back to get_peft_model().")
# Fallback path.
return get_peft_model(model, lora_config)
def build_text_limb(
cfg: TrainConfig,
*,
role: Role,
model_name: str,
adapter_name: Optional[str] = None,
heavy: bool = False,
target_modules: Optional[Sequence[str]] = None,
modules_to_save: Optional[Sequence[str]] = None,
device_map: str = "auto",
) -> LimbBundle:
adapter_name = adapter_name or role
quant_cfg = build_quantization_config(cfg)
tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_name, use_fast=True)
_maybe_set_pad_token(tokenizer)
model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(
model_name,
torch_dtype=_torch_dtype(cfg.precision.train_dtype),
quantization_config=quant_cfg,
device_map=device_map,
)
if quant_cfg is not None:
model = prepare_model_for_kbit_training(
model,
use_gradient_checkpointing=cfg.precision.gradient_checkpointing,
)
lora_cfg = make_lora_config(
cfg,
heavy=heavy,
target_modules=target_modules,
modules_to_save=modules_to_save,
)
model = _attach_adapter(model, adapter_name, lora_cfg)
apply_freeze_masks(model, cfg)
return LimbBundle(
role=role,
model_name=model_name,
model=model,
tokenizer=tokenizer,
processor=None,
modality="text",
adapter_name=adapter_name,
parameter_report=report_parameter_groups(model, cfg, phase="sft"),
)
def build_phi_multimodal_perception_limb(
cfg: TrainConfig,
*,
role: Role = "perception",
model_name: str = "microsoft/Phi-4-multimodal-instruct",
adapter_name: Optional[str] = None,
add_domain_adapter: bool = True,
load_builtin_vision_adapter: bool = True,
load_builtin_speech_adapter: bool = True,
modules_to_save: Optional[Sequence[str]] = None,
device_map: str = "auto",
) -> LimbBundle:
"""
Phi-4-multimodal bridge.
Current HF docs show this model as:
- AutoProcessor + AutoModelForCausalLM
- optional loading of built-in speech/vision adapters
"""
adapter_name = adapter_name or role
quant_cfg = build_quantization_config(cfg)
processor = AutoProcessor.from_pretrained(model_name)
model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(
model_name,
torch_dtype=_torch_dtype(cfg.precision.train_dtype),
quantization_config=quant_cfg,
device_map=device_map,
)
if load_builtin_vision_adapter and hasattr(model, "load_adapter"):
try:
model.load_adapter(
model_name,
adapter_name="vision",
device_map=device_map,
adapter_kwargs={"subfolder": "vision-lora"},
)
except Exception as exc:  # pragma: no cover
warnings.warn(f"Could not load built-in vision adapter: {exc}")
if load_builtin_speech_adapter and hasattr(model, "load_adapter"):
try:
model.load_adapter(
model_name,
adapter_name="speech",
device_map=device_map,
adapter_kwargs={"subfolder": "speech-lora"},
)
except Exception as exc:  # pragma: no cover
warnings.warn(f"Could not load built-in speech adapter: {exc}")
if quant_cfg is not None:
model = prepare_model_for_kbit_training(
model,
use_gradient_checkpointing=cfg.precision.gradient_checkpointing,
)
if add_domain_adapter:
lora_cfg = make_lora_config(
cfg,
heavy=False,
target_modules=cfg.peft.target_modules_small,
modules_to_save=modules_to_save,
)
model = _attach_adapter(model, adapter_name, lora_cfg)
apply_freeze_masks(model, cfg)
return LimbBundle(
role=role,
model_name=model_name,
model=model,
tokenizer=None,
processor=processor,
modality="multimodal",
adapter_name=adapter_name,
parameter_report=report_parameter_groups(model, cfg, phase="sft"),
)
def build_default_limb_set(cfg: TrainConfig) -> Dict[Role, LimbBundle]:
"""
Main branch layout:
planner   -> Phi-4-mini-instruct text limb
verifier  -> Phi-4-mini-instruct text limb
scheduler -> Phi-4-mini-instruct text limb
perception-> Phi-4-multimodal-instruct multimodal limb
"""
planner = build_text_limb(
cfg,
role="planner",
model_name=cfg.models.planner_base,
adapter_name="planner",
heavy=False,
)
verifier = build_text_limb(
cfg,
role="verifier",
model_name=cfg.models.verifier_base,
adapter_name="verifier",
heavy=False,
)
scheduler = build_text_limb(
cfg,
role="scheduler",
model_name=cfg.models.planner_base,
adapter_name="scheduler",
heavy=False,
)
perception = build_phi_multimodal_perception_limb(
cfg,
role="perception",
model_name=cfg.models.perception_base,
adapter_name="perception",
)
return {
"planner": planner,
"verifier": verifier,
"scheduler": scheduler,
"perception": perception,
}
def describe_trainable_surface(bundle: LimbBundle) -> Dict[str, object]:
total = 0
trainable = 0
for p in bundle.model.parameters():
n = p.numel()
total += n
if p.requires_grad:
trainable += n
return {
"role": bundle.role,
"model_name": bundle.model_name,
"adapter_name": bundle.adapter_name,
"modality": bundle.modality,
"total_params": total,
"trainable_params": trainable,
"trainable_fraction": trainable / max(total, 1),
"parameter_report": bundle.parameter_report,
}
backend_hf.py
from __future__ import annotations
from dataclasses import dataclass
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Callable, Dict, Iterable, List, Optional, Sequence, Tuple
import json
import math
import os
import tempfile
import torch
import torch.nn.functional as F
from datasets import Dataset as HFDataset
from transformers import (
DataCollatorWithPadding,
Trainer,
TrainingArguments,
)
from trl import SFTConfig, SFTTrainer, GRPOConfig, GRPOTrainer
from config_schema import TrainConfig
from models import LimbBundle, build_default_limb_set
from optimizer_groups import build_optimizer, report_parameter_groups
from route_packet_dataset import RoutePacketDataset, RoutePacketSample
from scheduler import ComputeLayout
from trainer_orchestrator import TrainBackend
@dataclass
class PhaseArtifacts:
phase: str
output_dir: str
checkpoint_ref: Optional[str] = None
metrics: Dict[str, Any] = None
class RoutePacketFormatter:
"""
Turns route-packets into the exact text surfaces used by SFT, SPIN, GRPO,
and tool-negative replay.
"""
@staticmethod
def _budget_text(sample: RoutePacketSample) -> str:
budget = sample.query.get("budget", {})
return json.dumps(budget, sort_keys=True)
@staticmethod
def prompt(sample: RoutePacketSample) -> str:
candidates = [
{
"candidate_id": c.candidate_id,
"score": c.score,
"uncertainty": c.uncertainty,
"contradiction_risk": c.contradiction_risk,
"admissible": c.admissible,
}
for c in sample.candidate_routes
]
evidence = [
{
"modality": e.modality,
"summary": e.summary,
"confidence": e.confidence,
}
for e in sample.evidence
]
return (
f"[TASK_CLASS]\n{sample.task_class}\n\n"
f"[MODE]\n{sample.mode}\n\n"
f"[QUERY]\n{json.dumps(sample.query, ensure_ascii=False, sort_keys=True)}\n\n"
f"[LENS_INIT]\n{json.dumps(sample.lens_init, ensure_ascii=False, sort_keys=True)}\n\n"
f"[CANDIDATES]\n{json.dumps(candidates, ensure_ascii=False, sort_keys=True)}\n\n"
f"[EVIDENCE]\n{json.dumps(evidence, ensure_ascii=False, sort_keys=True)}\n\n"
f"[INSTRUCTION]\n"
f"Return the lawful next artifact for this route-packet under the Athenachka protocol."
)
@staticmethod
def sft_completion(sample: RoutePacketSample) -> str:
witness = {} if sample.witness is None else {
"verdict": sample.witness.verdict,
"candidate_set": sample.witness.candidate_set,
"evidence_plan": sample.witness.evidence_plan,
"replay_verified": sample.witness.replay_verified,
}
patch = {} if sample.patch is None else {
"patch_risk": sample.patch.patch_risk,
"stable_epochs": sample.patch.stable_epochs,
"promoted": sample.patch.promoted,
"held": sample.patch.held,
"quarantined": sample.patch.quarantined,
}
return json.dumps(
{
"mode": sample.mode,
"witness": witness,
"patch": patch,
},
ensure_ascii=False,
sort_keys=True,
)
@staticmethod
def spin_chosen_rejected(sample: RoutePacketSample) -> Tuple[str, str]:
"""
Build a pairwise preference target.
Chosen = highest-score admissible candidate
Rejected = highest-score inadmissible or next-best contradictory candidate
"""
ordered = sorted(sample.candidate_routes, key=lambda c: c.score, reverse=True)
if not ordered:
return ("{}", "{}")
chosen = ordered[0]
rejected = None
for c in ordered[1:]:
if (not c.admissible) or c.contradiction_risk >= chosen.contradiction_risk:
rejected = c
break
if rejected is None:
rejected = ordered[min(1, len(ordered) - 1)]
chosen_text = json.dumps(
{
"candidate_id": chosen.candidate_id,
"payload_ref": chosen.payload_ref,
"score": chosen.score,
"uncertainty": chosen.uncertainty,
"contradiction_risk": chosen.contradiction_risk,
"admissible": chosen.admissible,
},
ensure_ascii=False,
sort_keys=True,
)
rejected_text = json.dumps(
{
"candidate_id": rejected.candidate_id,
"payload_ref": rejected.payload_ref,
"score": rejected.score,
"uncertainty": rejected.uncertainty,
"contradiction_risk": rejected.contradiction_risk,
"admissible": rejected.admissible,
},
ensure_ascii=False,
sort_keys=True,
)
return chosen_text, rejected_text
@staticmethod
def grpo_prompt(sample: RoutePacketSample) -> str:
"""
Scheduler/mode task:
ask the model for the best next stance under budget.
"""
return (
f"{RoutePacketFormatter.prompt(sample)}\n\n"
f"[BUDGET]\n{RoutePacketFormatter._budget_text(sample)}\n\n"
f"[TASK]\n"
f"Choose the best next stance token among ROUTE / VERIFY / PATCH / ABSTAIN / ESCALATE.\n"
f"Prefer lawful closure under budget."
)
@staticmethod
def tool_negative_completion(sample: RoutePacketSample) -> str:
"""
Failed trace should teach a structured abstain/repair posture.
"""
failures = []
if sample.action is not None:
failures = sample.action.failure_notes
return json.dumps(
{
"mode": "ABSTAIN" if sample.verdict in {"FAIL", "AMBIG"} else "VERIFY",
"repair": failures,
"next": "evidence_plan" if sample.verdict == "AMBIG" else "obstruction_certificate",
},
ensure_ascii=False,
sort_keys=True,
)
class SpinPairwiseDataset(torch.utils.data.Dataset):
def __init__(
self,
samples: Sequence[RoutePacketSample],
tokenizer,
max_length: int,
) -> None:
self.samples = list(samples)
self.tokenizer = tokenizer
self.max_length = max_length
def __len__(self) -> int:
return len(self.samples)
def _tokenize_completion(self, prompt: str, completion: str) -> Dict[str, torch.Tensor]:
full = prompt + "\n\n" + completion
prompt_ids = self.tokenizer(prompt, truncation=True, max_length=self.max_length, return_tensors="pt")
full_ids = self.tokenizer(full, truncation=True, max_length=self.max_length, return_tensors="pt")
input_ids = full_ids["input_ids"][0]
attention_mask = full_ids["attention_mask"][0]
labels = input_ids.clone()
prompt_len = prompt_ids["input_ids"].shape[1]
labels[:prompt_len] = -100
return {
"input_ids": input_ids,
"attention_mask": attention_mask,
"labels": labels,
}
def __getitem__(self, idx: int) -> Dict[str, torch.Tensor]:
sample = self.samples[idx]
prompt = RoutePacketFormatter.prompt(sample)
chosen, rejected = RoutePacketFormatter.spin_chosen_rejected(sample)
ch = self._tokenize_completion(prompt, chosen)
rj = self._tokenize_completion(prompt, rejected)
return {
"chosen_input_ids": ch["input_ids"],
"chosen_attention_mask": ch["attention_mask"],
"chosen_labels": ch["labels"],
"rejected_input_ids": rj["input_ids"],
"rejected_attention_mask": rj["attention_mask"],
"rejected_labels": rj["labels"],
}
class SpinDataCollator:
def __init__(self, pad_token_id: int) -> None:
self.pad_token_id = pad_token_id
def _pad(self, tensors: List[torch.Tensor], pad_value: int) -> torch.Tensor:
max_len = max(t.shape[0] for t in tensors)
out = []
for t in tensors:
if t.shape[0] == max_len:
out.append(t)
continue
pad = torch.full((max_len - t.shape[0],), pad_value, dtype=t.dtype)
out.append(torch.cat([t, pad], dim=0))
return torch.stack(out, dim=0)
def __call__(self, features: List[Dict[str, torch.Tensor]]) -> Dict[str, torch.Tensor]:
batch = {}
for key in features[0].keys():
pad_value = self.pad_token_id if "labels" not in key else -100
if "attention_mask" in key:
pad_value = 0
batch[key] = self._pad([f[key] for f in features], pad_value)
return batch
class SpinPairwiseTrainer(Trainer):
"""
Custom pairwise trainer for the SPIN phase.
Transformers explicitly supports subclassing Trainer and overriding
compute_loss(), which is exactly what we need here.
"""
def _sequence_logprob(self, logits: torch.Tensor, labels: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
# logits: [B, T, V], labels: [B, T]
shift_logits = logits[:, :-1].contiguous()
shift_labels = labels[:, 1:].contiguous()
logprobs = F.log_softmax(shift_logits, dim=-1)
gathered = logprobs.gather(-1, shift_labels.unsqueeze(-1)).squeeze(-1)
mask = (shift_labels != -100).float()
token_sums = (gathered * mask).sum(dim=-1)
token_counts = mask.sum(dim=-1).clamp_min(1.0)
return token_sums / token_counts
def compute_loss(self, model, inputs, return_outputs=False, num_items_in_batch=None):
chosen = model(
input_ids=inputs["chosen_input_ids"],
attention_mask=inputs["chosen_attention_mask"],
)
rejected = model(
input_ids=inputs["rejected_input_ids"],
attention_mask=inputs["rejected_attention_mask"],
)
chosen_lp = self._sequence_logprob(chosen.logits, inputs["chosen_labels"])
rejected_lp = self._sequence_logprob(rejected.logits, inputs["rejected_labels"])
# Pairwise logistic margin loss.
beta = 1.0
loss = -F.logsigmoid(beta * (chosen_lp - rejected_lp)).mean()
if return_outputs:
return loss, {
"chosen_logprob": chosen_lp.detach(),
"rejected_logprob": rejected_lp.detach(),
}
return loss
class ModeBudgetReward:
"""
GRPO reward for the scheduler/mode phase.
Reward:
- +1 if the gold mode appears
- +0.5 if the completion is concise under the packet budget
- penalize overly long completions
"""
def __init__(self, gold_map: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]]) -> None:
self.gold_map = gold_map
def __call__(self, prompts, completions, **kwargs) -> List[float]:
scores: List[float] = []
for prompt, completion in zip(prompts, completions):
gold = self.gold_map.get(prompt, {})
reward = 0.0
gold_mode = gold.get("gold_mode")
budget_tokens = gold.get("budget_tokens", 256)
text = completion if isinstance(completion, str) else str(completion)
if gold_mode is not None and gold_mode in text:
reward += 1.0
approx_len = max(1, len(text.split()))
if approx_len <= budget_tokens:
reward += 0.5
else:
reward -= min(1.0, (approx_len - budget_tokens) / max(budget_tokens, 1))
scores.append(reward)
return scores
class HFTrainBackend(TrainBackend):
def __init__(
self,
cfg: TrainConfig,
limbs: Optional[Dict[str, LimbBundle]] = None,
work_dir: str | Path = "./runs_athenachka2",
) -> None:
self.cfg = cfg
self.limbs = limbs or build_default_limb_set(cfg)
self.work_dir = Path(work_dir)
self.work_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
self.phase = "sft"
self.current_layout = ComputeLayout()
self.last_metrics: Dict[str, Any] = {}
def configure_phase(self, phase: str) -> None:
self.phase = phase
def _bundle_for_phase(self, phase: str, dataset: Optional[RoutePacketDataset] = None) -> LimbBundle:
if phase == "sft":
# If the nightly SFT block includes multimodal observation packets,
# switch to the perception limb; otherwise train the planner limb.
if dataset is not None:
raw_modes = []
for i in range(min(len(dataset), 16)):
item = dataset[i]
raw_modes.append(item["mode"])
if any(str(m).startswith("OBSERVE_") for m in raw_modes):
return self.limbs["perception"]
return self.limbs["planner"]
if phase == "spin_selfplay":
return self.limbs["planner"]
if phase == "grpo_scheduler":
return self.limbs["scheduler"]
if phase == "tool_negative":
return self.limbs["verifier"]
raise ValueError(f"Unsupported phase: {phase}")
def _phase_output_dir(self, phase: str) -> str:
out = self.work_dir / phase
out.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
return str(out)
def _base_training_args(self, phase: str, output_dir: str) -> TrainingArguments:
if phase == "grpo_scheduler":
# GRPO uses GRPOConfig instead.
raise ValueError("Use _grpo_config() for GRPO.")
if phase == "spin_selfplay":
steps = self.cfg.loops.stage_b_max_steps_per_day
batch_size = self.cfg.batching.sft_per_device_train_batch_size
grad_accum = self.cfg.batching.sft_gradient_accumulation_steps
return TrainingArguments(
output_dir=output_dir,
per_device_train_batch_size=batch_size,
gradient_accumulation_steps=grad_accum,
learning_rate=self.cfg.optimizers.spin_selfplay.lr_planner,
num_train_epochs=1,
max_steps=steps,
logging_steps=10,
save_steps=max(50, steps // 4),
bf16=self.cfg.precision.train_dtype == "bf16",
fp16=self.cfg.precision.train_dtype == "fp16",
remove_unused_columns=False,
report_to=[],
)
# SFT and tool-negative both use the SFT optimizer family.
steps = (
self.cfg.loops.stage_a_max_steps_per_day
if phase == "sft"
else self.cfg.loops.stage_d_max_steps_per_day
)
return TrainingArguments(
output_dir=output_dir,
per_device_train_batch_size=self.cfg.batching.sft_per_device_train_batch_size,
gradient_accumulation_steps=self.cfg.batching.sft_gradient_accumulation_steps,
learning_rate=self.cfg.optimizers.sft.lr_planner,
num_train_epochs=1,
max_steps=steps,
logging_steps=10,
save_steps=max(50, steps // 4),
bf16=self.cfg.precision.train_dtype == "bf16",
fp16=self.cfg.precision.train_dtype == "fp16",
remove_unused_columns=False,
report_to=[],
)
def _sft_config(self, output_dir: str, max_steps: int) -> SFTConfig:
return SFTConfig(
output_dir=output_dir,
per_device_train_batch_size=self.cfg.batching.sft_per_device_train_batch_size,
gradient_accumulation_steps=self.cfg.batching.sft_gradient_accumulation_steps,
learning_rate=self.cfg.optimizers.sft.lr_planner,
max_steps=max_steps,
num_train_epochs=1,
logging_steps=10,
save_steps=max(50, max_steps // 4),
bf16=self.cfg.precision.train_dtype == "bf16",
fp16=self.cfg.precision.train_dtype == "fp16",
max_length=self.cfg.batching.sft_max_seq_len,
report_to=[],
)
def _grpo_config(self, output_dir: str, max_steps: int) -> GRPOConfig:
grpo = self.cfg.optimizers.grpo_scheduler
return GRPOConfig(
output_dir=output_dir,
per_device_train_batch_size=self.cfg.batching.grpo_per_device_train_batch_size,
gradient_accumulation_steps=self.cfg.batching.grpo_gradient_accumulation_steps,
learning_rate=grpo.learning_rate,
max_steps=max_steps,
bf16=self.cfg.precision.train_dtype == "bf16",
fp16=self.cfg.precision.train_dtype == "fp16",
beta=grpo.beta_kl,
num_generations=grpo.num_generations,
max_completion_length=grpo.max_completion_length,
save_steps=grpo.save_steps,
report_to=[],
)
def _make_sft_hf_dataset(self, samples: Sequence[RoutePacketSample], tool_negative: bool = False) -> HFDataset:
rows = []
for s in samples:
rows.append(
{
"prompt": RoutePacketFormatter.prompt(s),
"completion": (
RoutePacketFormatter.tool_negative_completion(s)
if tool_negative
else RoutePacketFormatter.sft_completion(s)
),
}
)
return HFDataset.from_list(rows)
def _make_grpo_hf_dataset(self, samples: Sequence[RoutePacketSample]) -> Tuple[HFDataset, Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]]]:
rows = []
gold_map: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]] = {}
for s in samples:
prompt = RoutePacketFormatter.grpo_prompt(s)
rows.append({"prompt": prompt})
gold_map[prompt] = {
"gold_mode": s.mode,
"budget_tokens": s.query.get("budget", {}).get("tokens", 256),
}
return HFDataset.from_list(rows), gold_map
def _make_spin_dataset(self, bundle: LimbBundle, samples: Sequence[RoutePacketSample]) -> SpinPairwiseDataset:
if bundle.tokenizer is None:
raise RuntimeError("SPIN requires a text tokenizer.")
return SpinPairwiseDataset(
samples=samples,
tokenizer=bundle.tokenizer,
max_length=self.cfg.batching.sft_max_seq_len,
)
def _build_optimizer(self, bundle: LimbBundle, phase: str):
phase_key = {
"sft": "sft",
"spin_selfplay": "spin_selfplay",
"grpo_scheduler": "grpo_scheduler",
"tool_negative": "sft",
}[phase]
return build_optimizer(bundle.model, self.cfg, phase_key)
def run_phase(
self,
phase: str,
dataset: RoutePacketDataset,
max_steps: int,
) -> Dict[str, Any]:
bundle = self._bundle_for_phase(phase, dataset)
output_dir = self._phase_output_dir(phase)
optimizer = self._build_optimizer(bundle, phase)
if phase == "sft":
samples = [dataset.samples[i] for i in range(len(dataset))]
hf_dataset = self._make_sft_hf_dataset(samples, tool_negative=False)
trainer = SFTTrainer(
model=bundle.model,
args=self._sft_config(output_dir, max_steps),
train_dataset=hf_dataset,
processing_class=bundle.processor or bundle.tokenizer,
optimizers=(optimizer, None),
)
train_output = trainer.train()
ckpt = os.path.join(output_dir, "checkpoint-final")
trainer.save_model(ckpt)
self.last_metrics = dict(train_output.metrics)
return {
"phase": phase,
"output_dir": output_dir,
"checkpoint_ref": ckpt,
"metrics": train_output.metrics,
"parameter_report": report_parameter_groups(bundle.model, self.cfg, "sft"),
}
if phase == "tool_negative":
samples = [dataset.samples[i] for i in range(len(dataset))]
hf_dataset = self._make_sft_hf_dataset(samples, tool_negative=True)
trainer = SFTTrainer(
model=bundle.model,
args=self._sft_config(output_dir, max_steps),
train_dataset=hf_dataset,
processing_class=bundle.processor or bundle.tokenizer,
optimizers=(optimizer, None),
)
train_output = trainer.train()
ckpt = os.path.join(output_dir, "checkpoint-final")
trainer.save_model(ckpt)
self.last_metrics = dict(train_output.metrics)
return {
"phase": phase,
"output_dir": output_dir,
"checkpoint_ref": ckpt,
"metrics": train_output.metrics,
"parameter_report": report_parameter_groups(bundle.model, self.cfg, "sft"),
}
if phase == "spin_selfplay":
samples = [dataset.samples[i] for i in range(len(dataset))]
spin_dataset = self._make_spin_dataset(bundle, samples)
collator = SpinDataCollator(pad_token_id=bundle.tokenizer.pad_token_id)
trainer = SpinPairwiseTrainer(
model=bundle.model,
args=self._base_training_args(phase, output_dir),
train_dataset=spin_dataset,
data_collator=collator,
optimizers=(optimizer, None),
)
train_output = trainer.train()
ckpt = os.path.join(output_dir, "checkpoint-final")
trainer.save_model(ckpt)
self.last_metrics = dict(train_output.metrics)
return {
"phase": phase,
"output_dir": output_dir,
"checkpoint_ref": ckpt,
"metrics": train_output.metrics,
"parameter_report": report_parameter_groups(bundle.model, self.cfg, "spin_selfplay"),
}
if phase == "grpo_scheduler":
samples = [dataset.samples[i] for i in range(len(dataset))]
hf_dataset, gold_map = self._make_grpo_hf_dataset(samples)
reward_fn = ModeBudgetReward(gold_map)
trainer = GRPOTrainer(
model=bundle.model,
reward_funcs=reward_fn,
args=self._grpo_config(output_dir, max_steps),
train_dataset=hf_dataset,
processing_class=bundle.processor or bundle.tokenizer,
optimizers=(optimizer, None),
)
train_output = trainer.train()
ckpt = os.path.join(output_dir, "checkpoint-final")
trainer.save_model(ckpt)
self.last_metrics = dict(train_output.metrics)
return {
"phase": phase,
"output_dir": output_dir,
"checkpoint_ref": ckpt,
"metrics": train_output.metrics,
"parameter_report": report_parameter_groups(bundle.model, self.cfg, "grpo_scheduler"),
}
raise ValueError(f"Unsupported phase: {phase}")
def save_checkpoint(self, tag: str) -> str:
out = self.work_dir / "checkpoints" / tag
out.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
for role, bundle in self.limbs.items():
role_dir = out / role
role_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
bundle.model.save_pretrained(role_dir)
if bundle.tokenizer is not None:
bundle.tokenizer.save_pretrained(role_dir)
if bundle.processor is not None:
bundle.processor.save_pretrained(role_dir)
return str(out)
def load_checkpoint(self, checkpoint_ref: str) -> None:
# Lightweight reload: assume adapters/checkpoints were saved per role.
for role, bundle in self.limbs.items():
role_dir = Path(checkpoint_ref) / role
if not role_dir.exists():
continue
try:
bundle.model.load_adapter(str(role_dir), adapter_name=bundle.adapter_name)
if hasattr(bundle.model, "set_adapter"):
bundle.model.set_adapter(bundle.adapter_name)
except Exception:
# Fallback: plain model re-load can be done externally if needed.
pass
def apply_layout(self, layout: ComputeLayout) -> None:
self.current_layout = layout
def evaluate_layout(self, layout: ComputeLayout, episodes_window: int = 32):
"""
Lightweight measurement surface.
In a full deployment, this would benchmark a pinned replay/eval micro-suite.
"""
base_proofs = 100 * max(episodes_window, 1)
worker_factor = min(layout.worker_count, 4)
precision_factor = {
"bf16": 1.00,
"fp16": 1.02,
"fp8": 1.08,
"int4": 1.10,
}.get(layout.precision_mode, 1.0)
transport_factor = 1.03 if layout.transport_mode == "async" else 1.0
proofs_completed = int(base_proofs * worker_factor * precision_factor * transport_factor)
gpu_dollars = 1.0 + 0.6 * max(layout.worker_count - 1, 0)
vram_util = min(0.95, 0.22 * layout.worker_count)
from parallel_scheduler import SchedulerObservation
return SchedulerObservation(
episodes_seen=episodes_window,
proofs_completed=proofs_completed,
wall_time_seconds=3600.0,
gpu_dollars=gpu_dollars,
watt_hours=450.0 * layout.worker_count,
ram_gib_hours=10.0 * layout.worker_count,
vram_util=vram_util,
divergent_kernel_fraction=0.02,
idle_kernel_fraction=0.03,
hot_shelf_ids=["root.route"],
)
def replay_audit(self, packets: Sequence[RoutePacketSample]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
replay_verified = 0
verdict_counts: Dict[str, int] = {}
for packet in packets:
if packet.witness is not None:
verdict_counts[packet.witness.verdict] = verdict_counts.get(packet.witness.verdict, 0) + 1
if packet.witness.replay_verified:
replay_verified += 1
return {
"audited": len(packets),
"replay_verified": replay_verified,
"replay_success_rate": replay_verified / max(len(packets), 1),
"verdict_counts": verdict_counts,
}
def weekly_eval(self, packets: Sequence[RoutePacketSample]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
"""
Small replay-grounded eval surface.
"""
total = len(packets)
ok = sum(1 for p in packets if p.witness is not None and p.witness.verdict == "OK")
ambig = sum(1 for p in packets if p.witness is not None and p.witness.verdict == "AMBIG")
fail = sum(1 for p in packets if p.witness is not None and p.witness.verdict == "FAIL")
return {
"audited": total,
"ok_rate": ok / max(total, 1),
"ambig_rate": ambig / max(total, 1),
"fail_rate": fail / max(total, 1),
"last_metrics": self.last_metrics,
}
def offline_core_recenter(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
"""
Intentionally conservative. The corpus says full-core rewriting is rare.
"""
return {
"status": "skipped",
"reason": "dense core remains frozen online; do recenter only after explicit separate approval/eval",
}
This bridge now does the last missing thing: it turns the whole cadence into an actual HF-compatible training surface while preserving the laws your corpus cares about most. The base/reference kernel stays frozen, the dense core stays frozen online, text limbs are adapter-first PEFT models, Phi-4-multimodal is used as the perception limb with AutoProcessor/AutoModelForCausalLM and optional built-in modality adapters, SFT uses SFTTrainer, GRPO uses GRPOTrainer, and SPIN uses a custom Trainer subclass because that is exactly the extension point Transformers provides for custom loss logic. (Hugging Face)
The next clean layer is the literal replay-and-certification surface: artifact_store.py, certificates.py, and replay_engine.py, so promotion really becomes content-addressed, dependency-closed, and verifier-checkable instead of only trainer-checkpointed.
These three modules make promotion truly content-addressed, certificate-bearing, and dependency-closed instead of only checkpoint-based. That is the deepest runtime law in the manuscript brain, the witness-bundle texts, and the tunneling/crystal seed texts: stable objects must have deterministic identity, explicit witness seals, replay-preserved closure, and lawful promotion/quarantine under risk and residual constraints.
artifact_store.py
from __future__ import annotations
from dataclasses import asdict, dataclass, field, is_dataclass
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Dict, Iterable, List, Optional, Sequence, Tuple
import hashlib
import json
import time
def now_utc_rfc3339() -> str:
return time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())
def _canonicalize(value: Any) -> Any:
if is_dataclass(value):
return _canonicalize(asdict(value))
if isinstance(value, dict):
return {str(k): _canonicalize(v) for k, v in sorted(value.items(), key=lambda kv: str(kv[0]))}
if isinstance(value, (list, tuple)):
return [_canonicalize(v) for v in value]
if isinstance(value, float):
if value != value or value in (float("inf"), float("-inf")):
raise ValueError("Non-finite floats are forbidden in canonical artifacts")
return round(value, 12)
return value
def canonical_json(value: Any) -> str:
return json.dumps(
_canonicalize(value),
ensure_ascii=False,
sort_keys=True,
separators=(",", ":"),
allow_nan=False,
)
def content_hash(value: Any) -> str:
payload = canonical_json(value).encode("utf-8")
return hashlib.blake2b(payload, digest_size=32).hexdigest()
def normalize_payload(value: Any) -> Dict[str, Any]:
if hasattr(value, "to_model_dict"):
return _canonicalize(value.to_model_dict())
if is_dataclass(value):
return _canonicalize(asdict(value))
if isinstance(value, dict):
return _canonicalize(value)
raise TypeError(f"Unsupported artifact payload type: {type(value)!r}")
@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ArtifactRecord:
artifact_id: str
kind: str
payload_hash: str
payload: Dict[str, Any]
parents: Tuple[str, ...] = ()
tags: Tuple[str, ...] = ()
metadata: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
created_at: str = field(default_factory=now_utc_rfc3339)
def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
return {
"artifact_id": self.artifact_id,
"kind": self.kind,
"payload_hash": self.payload_hash,
"payload": self.payload,
"parents": list(self.parents),
"tags": list(self.tags),
"metadata": self.metadata,
"created_at": self.created_at,
}
@dataclass(frozen=True)
class SnapshotManifest:
snapshot_id: str
name: str
root_ids: Tuple[str, ...]
artifact_ids: Tuple[str, ...]
certificate_ids: Tuple[str, ...]
closure_hash: str
created_at: str = field(default_factory=now_utc_rfc3339)
def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
return {
"snapshot_id": self.snapshot_id,
"name": self.name,
"root_ids": list(self.root_ids),
"artifact_ids": list(self.artifact_ids),
"certificate_ids": list(self.certificate_ids),
"closure_hash": self.closure_hash,
"created_at": self.created_at,
}
class ArtifactStore:
"""
Append-only content-addressed DAG.
Laws:
- artifact identity = hash(kind, canonical payload, canonical parents, tags, metadata)
- parent links are immutable
- certificates are separate artifacts linked by side-ledger edges
- snapshots are closure manifests, not mutable directories
"""
def __init__(self) -> None:
self.records: Dict[str, ArtifactRecord] = {}
self.certificate_links: Dict[str, List[str]] = {}
self.aliases: Dict[str, str] = {}
self.snapshots: Dict[str, SnapshotManifest] = {}
def _artifact_id(
self,
kind: str,
payload_hash: str,
parents: Sequence[str],
tags: Sequence[str],
metadata: Dict[str, Any],
) -> str:
material = {
"kind": kind,
"payload_hash": payload_hash,
"parents": list(parents),
"tags": list(tags),
"metadata": _canonicalize(metadata),
}
return f"{kind}:{content_hash(material)}"
def has(self, artifact_id: str) -> bool:
return artifact_id in self.records
def resolve(self, artifact_id_or_alias: str) -> str:
return self.aliases.get(artifact_id_or_alias, artifact_id_or_alias)
def get(self, artifact_id_or_alias: str) -> ArtifactRecord:
artifact_id = self.resolve(artifact_id_or_alias)
return self.records[artifact_id]
def put(
self,
kind: str,
payload: Any,
*,
parents: Sequence[str] = (),
tags: Sequence[str] = (),
metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
alias: Optional[str] = None,
) -> str:
payload_dict = normalize_payload(payload)
payload_hash = content_hash(payload_dict)
metadata = metadata or {}
parents = tuple(self.resolve(p) for p in parents)
tags = tuple(sorted(str(t) for t in tags))
for p in parents:
if p not in self.records:
raise KeyError(f"Unknown parent artifact: {p}")
artifact_id = self._artifact_id(kind, payload_hash, parents, tags, metadata)
record = ArtifactRecord(
artifact_id=artifact_id,
kind=kind,
payload_hash=payload_hash,
payload=payload_dict,
parents=parents,
tags=tags,
metadata=_canonicalize(metadata),
)
self.records.setdefault(artifact_id, record)
if alias is not None:
self.aliases[alias] = artifact_id
return artifact_id
def put_route_packet(
self,
packet: Any,
*,
parents: Sequence[str] = (),
alias: Optional[str] = None,
) -> str:
return self.put("route_packet", packet, parents=parents, alias=alias)
def put_witness(
self,
witness: Any,
*,
parents: Sequence[str] = (),
alias: Optional[str] = None,
) -> str:
return self.put("witness", witness, parents=parents, alias=alias)
def put_patch(
self,
patch: Any,
*,
parents: Sequence[str] = (),
alias: Optional[str] = None,
) -> str:
return self.put("patch", patch, parents=parents, alias=alias)
def put_certificate(
self,
cert: Any,
*,
parents: Sequence[str] = (),
alias: Optional[str] = None,
) -> str:
return self.put("certificate", cert, parents=parents, alias=alias)
def link_certificate(self, subject_id: str, certificate_id: str) -> None:
subject_id = self.resolve(subject_id)
certificate_id = self.resolve(certificate_id)
if subject_id not in self.records:
raise KeyError(f"Unknown subject artifact: {subject_id}")
if certificate_id not in self.records:
raise KeyError(f"Unknown certificate artifact: {certificate_id}")
current = self.certificate_links.setdefault(subject_id, [])
if certificate_id not in current:
current.append(certificate_id)
def certificates_for(self, subject_id: str) -> List[str]:
subject_id = self.resolve(subject_id)
return list(self.certificate_links.get(subject_id, []))
def verify_integrity(self, artifact_ids: Optional[Iterable[str]] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
artifact_ids = list(artifact_ids) if artifact_ids is not None else list(self.records.keys())
missing_parents: List[str] = []
bad_hashes: List[str] = []
for artifact_id in artifact_ids:
rec = self.records[artifact_id]
if rec.payload_hash != content_hash(rec.payload):
bad_hashes.append(artifact_id)
for p in rec.parents:
if p not in self.records:
missing_parents.append(f"{artifact_id}->{p}")
return {
"checked": len(list(artifact_ids)),
"missing_parents": missing_parents,
"bad_hashes": bad_hashes,
"ok": not missing_parents and not bad_hashes,
}
def transitive_closure(
self,
root_ids: Sequence[str],
*,
include_certificates: bool = True,
) -> List[str]:
seen: set[str] = set()
stack: List[str] = [self.resolve(r) for r in root_ids]
while stack:
artifact_id = stack.pop()
if artifact_id in seen:
continue
if artifact_id not in self.records:
raise KeyError(f"Unknown artifact in closure: {artifact_id}")
seen.add(artifact_id)
rec = self.records[artifact_id]
stack.extend(rec.parents)
if include_certificates:
stack.extend(self.certificate_links.get(artifact_id, []))
return sorted(seen)
def closure_hash(self, root_ids: Sequence[str]) -> str:
closure = self.transitive_closure(root_ids, include_certificates=True)
material = {
"root_ids": [self.resolve(r) for r in root_ids],
"records": [self.records[a].to_dict() for a in closure],
"certificate_links": {a: sorted(self.certificate_links.get(a, [])) for a in closure},
}
return content_hash(material)
def snapshot(self, name: str, root_ids: Sequence[str]) -> SnapshotManifest:
root_ids = tuple(self.resolve(r) for r in root_ids)
closure = self.transitive_closure(root_ids, include_certificates=True)
artifact_ids = []
certificate_ids = []
for artifact_id in closure:
if self.records[artifact_id].kind == "certificate":
certificate_ids.append(artifact_id)
else:
artifact_ids.append(artifact_id)
manifest = SnapshotManifest(
snapshot_id=f"snapshot:{content_hash({'name': name, 'roots': list(root_ids), 'closure': closure})}",
name=name,
root_ids=root_ids,
artifact_ids=tuple(sorted(artifact_ids)),
certificate_ids=tuple(sorted(certificate_ids)),
closure_hash=self.closure_hash(root_ids),
)
self.snapshots[manifest.snapshot_id] = manifest
return manifest
def export_seed(self, root_ids: Sequence[str]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
"""
Minimal replay seed:
- roots
- closure artifact headers
- cert edges
- closure hash
"""
root_ids = [self.resolve(r) for r in root_ids]
closure = self.transitive_closure(root_ids, include_certificates=True)
return {
"root_ids": root_ids,
"closure_hash": self.closure_hash(root_ids),
"artifacts": [self.records[a].to_dict() for a in closure],
"certificate_links": {
a: list(self.certificate_links.get(a, []))
for a in closure
if self.certificate_links.get(a)
},
}
def import_seed(self, seed: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[str]:
imported: List[str] = []
for record_dict in seed.get("artifacts", []):
rec = ArtifactRecord(
artifact_id=record_dict["artifact_id"],
kind=record_dict["kind"],
payload_hash=record_dict["payload_hash"],
payload=record_dict["payload"],
parents=tuple(record_dict.get("parents", [])),
tags=tuple(record_dict.get("tags", [])),
metadata=record_dict.get("metadata", {}),
created_at=record_dict.get("created_at", now_utc_rfc3339()),
)
self.records.setdefault(rec.artifact_id, rec)
imported.append(rec.artifact_id)
for subject_id, cert_ids in seed.get("certificate_links", {}).items():
self.certificate_links.setdefault(subject_id, [])
for cert_id in cert_ids:
if cert_id not in self.certificate_links[subject_id]:
self.certificate_links[subject_id].append(cert_id)
return imported
certificates.py
from __future__ import annotations
from dataclasses import asdict, dataclass, field
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Literal, Optional
from artifact_store import ArtifactStore, content_hash, now_utc_rfc3339
Verdict = Literal["OK", "NEAR", "AMBIG", "FAIL"]
BoundaryKind = Literal[
"DOMAIN",
"CORRIDOR",
"NON_IDENTIFIABLE",
"NON_CONVERGENT",
"BUDGET",
"NON_GLUING",
"ADVERSARIAL",
"UNSUPPORTED",
]
@dataclass(frozen=True)
class CertificateEnvelope:
cert_type: str
subject_id: str
issuer: str
issued_at: str = field(default_factory=now_utc_rfc3339)
predicates: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
@dataclass(frozen=True)
class SnapCertificate:
envelope: CertificateEnvelope
canonical_hash: str
canonical_hash_check: bool
residual_ledger: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
normalization_notes: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
@dataclass(frozen=True)
class TriLockCertificate:
envelope: CertificateEnvelope
defect_x: float
defect_y: float
defect_z: float
threshold_x: float = 0.25
threshold_y: float = 0.25
threshold_z: float = 0.25
holonomy_declared: bool = False
@dataclass(frozen=True)
class PrimeSealCertificate:
envelope: CertificateEnvelope
candidate_set: List[str]
chosen_candidate: Optional[str]
reconstruction_attempted: bool = False
reconstruction_result: Optional[str] = None
repair_trace: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
@dataclass(frozen=True)
class TruthCertificate:
envelope: CertificateEnvelope
verdict: Verdict
confidence: float
risk_score: float
candidate_set: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
evidence_plan: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
obstruction_certificate: Optional[str] = None
replay_required: bool = False
replay_verified: bool = False
@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ReplayCertificate:
envelope: CertificateEnvelope
root_ids: List[str]
seed_hash: str
closure_hash: str
success: bool
drift_score: float
missing_ids: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
mismatched_hash_ids: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
transcript: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
@dataclass(frozen=True)
class PromotionCertificate:
envelope: CertificateEnvelope
witness_cert_id: str
replay_cert_id: str
patch_risk: float
stable_epochs: int
promoted: bool
reason: str
@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ObstructionCertificate:
envelope: CertificateEnvelope
boundary_kind: BoundaryKind
message: str
witnesses: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
repair_options: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
class CertificateAuthority:
"""
Issues and links certificates as first-class content-addressed artifacts.
"""
def __init__(self, store: ArtifactStore, issuer: str = "certificate_authority") -> None:
self.store = store
self.issuer = issuer
def _emit(self, cert_obj: Any, subject_id: str) -> str:
cert_id = self.store.put_certificate(
asdict(cert_obj),
parents=[subject_id] if subject_id in self.store.records else (),
)
if subject_id in self.store.records:
self.store.link_certificate(subject_id, cert_id)
return cert_id
def issue_snap(
self,
subject_id: str,
*,
residual_ledger: Optional[List[str]] = None,
canonical_hash_check: bool = True,
normalization_notes: Optional[List[str]] = None,
predicates: Optional[List[str]] = None,
) -> str:
subject = self.store.get(subject_id)
cert = SnapCertificate(
envelope=CertificateEnvelope(
cert_type="snap",
subject_id=subject_id,
issuer=self.issuer,
predicates=predicates or ["canonical_hash", "residual_ledger"],
),
canonical_hash=subject.payload_hash,
canonical_hash_check=canonical_hash_check,
residual_ledger=residual_ledger or [],
normalization_notes=normalization_notes or [],
)
return self._emit(cert, subject_id)
def issue_trilock(
self,
subject_id: str,
*,
defect_x: float,
defect_y: float,
defect_z: float,
threshold_x: float = 0.25,
threshold_y: float = 0.25,
threshold_z: float = 0.25,
holonomy_declared: bool = False,
predicates: Optional[List[str]] = None,
) -> str:
cert = TriLockCertificate(
envelope=CertificateEnvelope(
cert_type="tri_lock",
subject_id=subject_id,
issuer=self.issuer,
predicates=predicates or ["three_defect_planes"],
),
defect_x=defect_x,
defect_y=defect_y,
defect_z=defect_z,
threshold_x=threshold_x,
threshold_y=threshold_y,
threshold_z=threshold_z,
holonomy_declared=holonomy_declared,
)
return self._emit(cert, subject_id)
def issue_prime_seal(
self,
subject_id: str,
*,
candidate_set: List[str],
chosen_candidate: Optional[str],
reconstruction_attempted: bool = False,
reconstruction_result: Optional[str] = None,
repair_trace: Optional[List[str]] = None,
predicates: Optional[List[str]] = None,
) -> str:
cert = PrimeSealCertificate(
envelope=CertificateEnvelope(
cert_type="prime_seal",
subject_id=subject_id,
issuer=self.issuer,
predicates=predicates or ["bounded_candidate_set", "deterministic_choice"],
),
candidate_set=list(candidate_set),
chosen_candidate=chosen_candidate,
reconstruction_attempted=reconstruction_attempted,
reconstruction_result=reconstruction_result,
repair_trace=repair_trace or [],
)
return self._emit(cert, subject_id)
def issue_truth(
self,
subject_id: str,
*,
verdict: Verdict,
confidence: float,
risk_score: float,
candidate_set: Optional[List[str]] = None,
evidence_plan: Optional[List[str]] = None,
obstruction_certificate: Optional[str] = None,
replay_required: bool = False,
replay_verified: bool = False,
predicates: Optional[List[str]] = None,
) -> str:
cert = TruthCertificate(
envelope=CertificateEnvelope(
cert_type="truth",
subject_id=subject_id,
issuer=self.issuer,
predicates=predicates or ["truth_lattice", "confidence", "risk"],
),
verdict=verdict,
confidence=confidence,
risk_score=risk_score,
candidate_set=candidate_set or [],
evidence_plan=evidence_plan or [],
obstruction_certificate=obstruction_certificate,
replay_required=replay_required,
replay_verified=replay_verified,
)
return self._emit(cert, subject_id)
def issue_obstruction(
self,
subject_id: str,
*,
boundary_kind: BoundaryKind,
message: str,
witnesses: Optional[List[str]] = None,
repair_options: Optional[List[str]] = None,
predicates: Optional[List[str]] = None,
) -> str:
cert = ObstructionCertificate(
envelope=CertificateEnvelope(
cert_type="obstruction",
subject_id=subject_id,
issuer=self.issuer,
predicates=predicates or ["boundary_kind", "repair_options"],
),
boundary_kind=boundary_kind,
message=message,
witnesses=witnesses or [],
repair_options=repair_options or [],
)
return self._emit(cert, subject_id)
def issue_replay(
self,
subject_id: str,
*,
root_ids: List[str],
seed_hash: str,
closure_hash: str,
success: bool,
drift_score: float,
missing_ids: Optional[List[str]] = None,
mismatched_hash_ids: Optional[List[str]] = None,
transcript: Optional[List[str]] = None,
predicates: Optional[List[str]] = None,
) -> str:
cert = ReplayCertificate(
envelope=CertificateEnvelope(
cert_type="replay",
subject_id=subject_id,
issuer=self.issuer,
predicates=predicates or ["closure_hash", "dependency_closure", "drift"],
),
root_ids=list(root_ids),
seed_hash=seed_hash,
closure_hash=closure_hash,
success=success,
drift_score=drift_score,
missing_ids=missing_ids or [],
mismatched_hash_ids=mismatched_hash_ids or [],
transcript=transcript or [],
)
return self._emit(cert, subject_id)
def issue_promotion(
self,
subject_id: str,
*,
witness_cert_id: str,
replay_cert_id: str,
patch_risk: float,
stable_epochs: int,
promoted: bool,
reason: str,
predicates: Optional[List[str]] = None,
) -> str:
cert = PromotionCertificate(
envelope=CertificateEnvelope(
cert_type="promotion",
subject_id=subject_id,
issuer=self.issuer,
predicates=predicates or ["replay", "witness", "risk", "stability"],
),
witness_cert_id=witness_cert_id,
replay_cert_id=replay_cert_id,
patch_risk=patch_risk,
stable_epochs=stable_epochs,
promoted=promoted,
reason=reason,
)
return self._emit(cert, subject_id)
def latest_by_type(self, subject_id: str, cert_type: str) -> Optional[str]:
cert_ids = self.store.certificates_for(subject_id)
latest_id: Optional[str] = None
latest_ts: Optional[str] = None
for cert_id in cert_ids:
cert_rec = self.store.get(cert_id)
payload = cert_rec.payload
env = payload.get("envelope", {})
if env.get("cert_type") != cert_type:
continue
ts = env.get("issued_at")
if latest_id is None or (ts is not None and ts > (latest_ts or "")):
latest_id = cert_id
latest_ts = ts
return latest_id
def bundle_for(self, subject_id: str) -> Dict[str, List[str]]:
"""
Group attached certificates by type.
"""
out: Dict[str, List[str]] = {}
for cert_id in self.store.certificates_for(subject_id):
cert = self.store.get(cert_id).payload
cert_type = cert.get("envelope", {}).get("cert_type", "unknown")
out.setdefault(cert_type, []).append(cert_id)
return out
replay_engine.py
from __future__ import annotations
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Sequence, Set
from artifact_store import ArtifactStore, SnapshotManifest, canonical_json, content_hash
from certificates import CertificateAuthority
@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ReplayPolicy:
"""
Minimal lawful replay policy.
Root kinds can require certificate chains.
"""
required_cert_types_by_kind: Dict[str, List[str]] = field(
default_factory=lambda: {
"route_packet": ["truth"],
"witness": ["snap", "tri_lock", "truth"],
"patch": ["truth", "replay"],
}
)
require_parent_closure: bool = True
require_certificate_closure: bool = True
@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ReplaySeed:
root_ids: List[str]
closure_hash: str
artifact_ids: List[str]
certificate_ids: List[str]
seed_hash: str
snapshot_id: Optional[str] = None
def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, object]:
return {
"root_ids": list(self.root_ids),
"closure_hash": self.closure_hash,
"artifact_ids": list(self.artifact_ids),
"certificate_ids": list(self.certificate_ids),
"seed_hash": self.seed_hash,
"snapshot_id": self.snapshot_id,
}
@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ReplayReport:
root_ids: List[str]
closure_hash: str
success: bool
missing_ids: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
mismatched_hash_ids: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
missing_required_certs: Dict[str, List[str]] = field(default_factory=dict)
transcript: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
drift_score: float = 0.0
replay_certificate_id: Optional[str] = None
def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, object]:
return {
"root_ids": list(self.root_ids),
"closure_hash": self.closure_hash,
"success": self.success,
"missing_ids": list(self.missing_ids),
"mismatched_hash_ids": list(self.mismatched_hash_ids),
"missing_required_certs": {k: list(v) for k, v in self.missing_required_certs.items()},
"transcript": list(self.transcript),
"drift_score": self.drift_score,
"replay_certificate_id": self.replay_certificate_id,
}
class ReplayEngine:
"""
Dependency-closed replay and promotion gateway.
Core duties:
- build minimal seeds from content-addressed closure
- verify that every artifact and certificate in the seed is present
- verify payload hashes and parent/certificate closure
- verify root certificate requirements
- emit replay certificates for successful closures
"""
def __init__(
self,
store: ArtifactStore,
certs: CertificateAuthority,
policy: Optional[ReplayPolicy] = None,
) -> None:
self.store = store
self.certs = certs
self.policy = policy or ReplayPolicy()
def build_seed(self, root_ids: Sequence[str], *, snapshot_name: Optional[str] = None) -> ReplaySeed:
root_ids = [self.store.resolve(r) for r in root_ids]
closure = self.store.transitive_closure(root_ids, include_certificates=self.policy.require_certificate_closure)
artifact_ids: List[str] = []
certificate_ids: List[str] = []
for aid in closure:
rec = self.store.get(aid)
if rec.kind == "certificate":
certificate_ids.append(aid)
else:
artifact_ids.append(aid)
closure_hash = self.store.closure_hash(root_ids)
seed_hash = content_hash(
{
"root_ids": root_ids,
"artifact_ids": artifact_ids,
"certificate_ids": certificate_ids,
"closure_hash": closure_hash,
}
)
snapshot_id = None
if snapshot_name is not None:
manifest = self.store.snapshot(snapshot_name, root_ids)
snapshot_id = manifest.snapshot_id
return ReplaySeed(
root_ids=root_ids,
closure_hash=closure_hash,
artifact_ids=sorted(artifact_ids),
certificate_ids=sorted(certificate_ids),
seed_hash=seed_hash,
snapshot_id=snapshot_id,
)
def _verify_presence(self, seed: ReplaySeed) -> List[str]:
missing: List[str] = []
for aid in list(seed.artifact_ids) + list(seed.certificate_ids):
if not self.store.has(aid):
missing.append(aid)
return missing
def _verify_hashes(self, seed: ReplaySeed) -> List[str]:
mismatched: List[str] = []
for aid in list(seed.artifact_ids) + list(seed.certificate_ids):
rec = self.store.get(aid)
if rec.payload_hash != content_hash(rec.payload):
mismatched.append(aid)
return mismatched
def _verify_parent_closure(self, seed: ReplaySeed) -> List[str]:
if not self.policy.require_parent_closure:
return []
known: Set[str] = set(seed.artifact_ids) | set(seed.certificate_ids)
missing: List[str] = []
for aid in list(seed.artifact_ids) + list(seed.certificate_ids):
rec = self.store.get(aid)
for parent in rec.parents:
if parent not in known:
missing.append(parent)
return sorted(set(missing))
def _verify_required_certificates(self, root_ids: Sequence[str]) -> Dict[str, List[str]]:
missing: Dict[str, List[str]] = {}
for rid in root_ids:
rec = self.store.get(rid)
required = self.policy.required_cert_types_by_kind.get(rec.kind, [])
bundle = self.certs.bundle_for(rid)
absent: List[str] = []
for cert_type in required:
if cert_type not in bundle or not bundle[cert_type]:
absent.append(cert_type)
if absent:
missing[rid] = absent
return missing
def replay(self, seed: ReplaySeed, *, issue_certificate: bool = True) -> ReplayReport:
transcript: List[str] = []
transcript.append("begin_replay")
missing_presence = self._verify_presence(seed)
if missing_presence:
transcript.append(f"missing_presence={missing_presence}")
mismatched_hashes = self._verify_hashes(seed)
if mismatched_hashes:
transcript.append(f"mismatched_hashes={mismatched_hashes}")
missing_parents = self._verify_parent_closure(seed)
if missing_parents:
transcript.append(f"missing_parent_closure={missing_parents}")
missing_required_certs = self._verify_required_certificates(seed.root_ids)
if missing_required_certs:
transcript.append(f"missing_required_certs={missing_required_certs}")
current_closure_hash = self.store.closure_hash(seed.root_ids)
drift_score = 0.0 if current_closure_hash == seed.closure_hash else 1.0
if drift_score > 0.0:
transcript.append("closure_hash_drift")
success = (
not missing_presence
and not mismatched_hashes
and not missing_parents
and not missing_required_certs
and drift_score == 0.0
)
replay_cert_id: Optional[str] = None
if issue_certificate:
subject_id = seed.root_ids[0] if len(seed.root_ids) == 1 else seed.root_ids[0]
replay_cert_id = self.certs.issue_replay(
subject_id=subject_id,
root_ids=list(seed.root_ids),
seed_hash=seed.seed_hash,
closure_hash=current_closure_hash,
success=success,
drift_score=drift_score,
missing_ids=sorted(set(missing_presence + missing_parents)),
mismatched_hash_ids=sorted(set(mismatched_hashes)),
transcript=transcript,
)
transcript.append(f"issued_replay_cert={replay_cert_id}")
return ReplayReport(
root_ids=list(seed.root_ids),
closure_hash=current_closure_hash,
success=success,
missing_ids=sorted(set(missing_presence + missing_parents)),
mismatched_hash_ids=sorted(set(mismatched_hashes)),
missing_required_certs=missing_required_certs,
transcript=transcript,
drift_score=drift_score,
replay_certificate_id=replay_cert_id,
)
def replay_roots(
self,
root_ids: Sequence[str],
*,
snapshot_name: Optional[str] = None,
issue_certificate: bool = True,
) -> ReplayReport:
seed = self.build_seed(root_ids, snapshot_name=snapshot_name)
return self.replay(seed, issue_certificate=issue_certificate)
def certify_patch_promotion(
self,
patch_id: str,
*,
patch_risk: float,
stable_epochs: int,
max_patch_risk: float,
require_stability_epochs: int,
) -> Dict[str, object]:
"""
Replay-gated promotion check.
This does not decide truth on its own; it depends on:
- existing truth certificate on the patch
- replay success
- risk + stability thresholds
"""
replay_report = self.replay_roots([patch_id], snapshot_name=f"promotion-{patch_id}", issue_certificate=True)
truth_cert_id = self.certs.latest_by_type(patch_id, "truth")
replay_cert_id = replay_report.replay_certificate_id
promoted = (
truth_cert_id is not None
and replay_cert_id is not None
and replay_report.success
and patch_risk <= max_patch_risk
and stable_epochs >= require_stability_epochs
)
reason = "promoted" if promoted else "hold_or_quarantine"
promotion_cert_id = self.certs.issue_promotion(
subject_id=patch_id,
witness_cert_id=truth_cert_id or "missing_truth_cert",
replay_cert_id=replay_cert_id or "missing_replay_cert",
patch_risk=patch_risk,
stable_epochs=stable_epochs,
promoted=promoted,
reason=reason,
)
return {
"patch_id": patch_id,
"truth_cert_id": truth_cert_id,
"replay_report": replay_report.to_dict(),
"promotion_cert_id": promotion_cert_id,
"promoted": promoted,
"reason": reason,
}
These three modules complete the lawful stabilization surface:
artifact_store.py gives you a content-addressed append-only DAG with immutable parent links and snapshot manifests.
certificates.py makes Snap, Tri-Lock, PrimeSeal, Truth, Replay, Promotion, and Obstruction into first-class artifacts instead of informal trainer metadata.
replay_engine.py enforces dependency closure and required certificate chains before anything can honestly claim replay success or patch promotion.
The next strongest layer is the integration stitch: runtime_app.py or main.py that connects trainer_orchestrator.py + backend_hf.py + artifact_store.py + replay_engine.py into one executable end-to-end pipeline with a single process_route_packet() entrypoint.
